< Text>
The best Carnitas Tacos anywhere from Turlock to Modesto!  Amazing toasted Corn flavor in the tortillas, the Carnitas have a nice texture due to the way they prepare the meat, they're always juicy and tender.  You get a tremendous value for your money.  The staff is very nice.  I highly recommend Tacos Mexico!</Text>

< Text>
My favorite Taco Truck in Turlock. Their Al Pastor Burrito Supreme is my favorite. The meat is perfectly season and it has the right amount of beans and rice. The salsa has just enough spice to not over power the taste buds. They take debit/credit cars which is a plus as I hardly ever carry cash. Their tacos are pretty good too. They provide quick service and are conveniently located. Try them out, you won't be disappointed.< /Text>

< text>
We were looking for something to eat in Pacific Grove with everything in town ( it was a friday night) seemed loaded with people, but Max's grill was less busy than anything we strolled past.  We chocked it up to their being located on a side street and it was to our luck of the night as we soon came to realize with our meal choices and service.

The wait staff was very friendly, attentive and service was quick. We received fresh bread with dipping oil immediately upon being seated so being the bread lover that I am and a hungry gal I was happy to partake.

I ordered the 'Fish of the Day' Salmon with pesto sauce, seasonal veggies and potatoes and my husband the other 'Fish of the Day' special Swordfish that I quickly swapped plates that became my dinner for the night. LOL

The Swordfish was cooked to perfection with an absolute delicate matching sauce that melted in my mouth.  This dish as the other also came with seasonal veggies and potatoes that were just the right amount and seasoned enough to let the true flavors shine through.  My husband and I shared the Garden salad that was perfectly balanced with a house made dressing, drizzled over the freshest greens.  I will say this was a wonderful dinner start to finish with my bubbly Prosecco to compliment my dinner wonderfully.

Max's Grill is a cozy restaurant that made for a lovely evening with delicious food on our October getaway.  Thank you again to the staff and Max's Grill - Enjoy!< /text>

<Rate>5<//Rate><review>We frequent PG (5-6 times a year) just to get away from the Bay Area eat race. We have amour favorite restaurants and this place just made our top list.

It has a quaint family atmosphere and the staff (the lander and a server) were super friendly. Our server Christian was knowledgeable about the menu and answered our questions in detail.

For the appetizer, we ordered tempura sand dab and it set the bar very high.  It was battered and seasoned perfectly and the fish was flaky and light.

I ordered the short ribs and I will have to say that it's one of the BEST meals I've had in the area. The meat literally melts in your mouth and did not have a lot of fat. The vegetables and potato au gratin were cooked perfectly but the sauce was the highlight. It was creamy, had layers of flavors and piping hot.

My wife ordered the fresh made ravioli stuffed with porcini and shiitake mushrooms and bri cheese topped with herb butter sauce. She absolutely loved it!

If you're in the area and are looking for a great place to eat with the atmosphere to match, then try this place. You won't be disappointed.

We will definitely be back!< /review><pictures>None< /pictures>< Resp>

<Pictures>None<//Pictures><name>Christina Black<//name><response>None<//response><Gmap_id>0x808de14ea6f0aaed:0xd668dbe42d7ae31<//Gmap_id><rate>5< /rate><Date>1578239928485< /Date><review>A really nice find.  The name is misleading, the menu isn't grill-centric. It's actually a sophisticated high cuisine menu at a relatively modest price.  I say "relatively modest" because there isn't much in the area that is cheap.  I sense that the chef wants to run a French-Asian fusion restaurant but because of customer demand and seafood sourcing in the area he's gone with a general European-Asian cuisine.  Ergo, cioppino is on the menu.  I love cioppino and so tried it out.  The ingredients were fresh and plentiful but it wasn't in the style of the big bowl soup cioppino stuffed with seafood a la Moneterey Fish House or Moss Landing's Phil's Fish Market.  Instead it is more of a deep plate cioppino with a sweat taste to the broth.  I really enjoyed it but wouldn't be able to eat any more than they served because of the sweetness.  Highly recommend the crab cakes which was almost all crab with a nice crisp outer shell.  One person in our group had the fixed menu.  The mushroom soup was amazing, the sand dabs was only ok and the creme brule wasn't good.

Overall, we had a nice experience and the service was excellent.< /review></record></dataset><record>
